    &lt;!--
		function topIdCheck(checkEl){
		    var objId = checkEl.id;
		    var checkObj = document.getElementById(objId);
		    var checkImgURI = checkObj.src;
		
		    if(checkImgURI.indexOf("checkBox_check.gif") == -1 ) {
		        checkObj.src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'checked'");
		    }else {
		        checkObj.src ="images/common/checkBox.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'unchecked'");
		    }
		}


        var saveChkVal = 'unchecked';
        
        function login(){
            var userId = trim(document.loginForm.userId.value);
            var password = trim(document.loginForm.password.value); 
            var msg = "";
            if(userId.length == 0){
                msg +="아이디를 입력하세요.\n";
            }
            if(password.length == 0 &amp;&amp; msg.length == 0){
                msg +="비밀번호를 입력하세요.";
            }
            
            if(msg.length &gt; 0){
                alert(msg);
            }else{
            	var saveChkImg = document.getElementById("saveChk");
		    	if(saveChkImg.src.indexOf('_check') &gt; 0){
		    		document.loginForm.saveChkYN.value = "Y";
		    	}
                document.loginForm.submit();
            }
        }
        
        function formsubmit(evt){
            var evt = window.event || evt;
            var evCode = ( window.netscape ) ? evt.which : evt.keyCode ;
            if(evCode == 13)
                login();
        }
        
        function setCookieId(){
            if(getCookie('betman.userId') != null &amp;&amp; getCookie('betman.userId') !='null'){
                document.loginForm.userId.value = getCookie('betman.userId');
                outerLoginFocus(document.getElementById('input_id'));
                document.getElementById("saveChk").src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
                saveChkVal = 'checked';
            }
        }
        
        setCookieId();

    //--&gt;
    </script>
<link href="css/navi.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
<script type="text/javascript">

    	var menuCode = "MN010100";
    	var naviMenuId;
    	var naviMenuIdSub;
    	try{
			naviMenuId = Number(menuCode.substring(2, 4)) - 1;
   			naviMenuIdSub = Number(menuCode.substring(4, 6)) - 1;
		}catch(e){
			naviMenuId = -1;
			naviMenuIdSub = -1;
		}finally{
			if(naviMenuId &gt; 3){
				naviMenuId = -1;
				naviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
		}
		

    	var overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
    	var overNaviMenuIdSub = naviMenuIdSub;
    	var isTimer = false;
    	var naviTimer;
    	
    	$(function(){

			if(naviMenuId &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; naviMenuIdSub &gt; -1){
				if(overNaviMenuId == naviMenuId){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				
				document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).getElementsByTagName("li")[naviMenuIdSub].className = "item02 selected";
			}
		});
		
		function topNaviController1(id, animated){

			if(animated){
				if(id != overNaviMenuId){
					if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
						document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
						document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
					}
					
					document.getElementById("ncg" + id).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + id).className = "depth02 depth020" + (id + 1) + " selected";
					
					overNaviMenuId = id;
					overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
				}
			}else{
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);

				}
				overNaviMenuId = -1;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function defNaviTop(){
    		if(naviMenuId != overNaviMenuId){
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
				}
				if(naviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function cancelHide(){
			clearTimeout(naviTimer);
			isTimer = false;
		}
    	
    	function hideTop(){
    		if(!isTimer){
    			isTimer = true;
    			naviTimer = setTimeout("defNaviTop()", 500);
    		}
    	}
		
    </script>

	function clickGameTab(tapSeq,whereStr) {
       var tapUrl = '';
       if (tapSeq == '1') {
           tapUrl = 'gameBuyGuide.so?gameId=G101';
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '2') {

                tapUrl = 'teamMatchRecord.so?method=getMatchRecordList&amp;gameId=G101&amp;innerRound=180056&amp;outerRound=56&amp;saleYear=2018';
           } else {

           }
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '7') {
    	      	   
       	   
    	   
           tapUrl = 'gameNoticeList.so?gameId=G101&amp;gameOutRound=2018/56';
           
           
       }
       
       clickGambetTab(tapSeq, tapUrl);
    }
        
	function clickWorldcupGameTab(tapSeq,whereStr) {
       var tapUrl = '';
       if (tapSeq == '1') {
           tapUrl = 'gameBuyGuide.so?gameId=G101';
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '2') {
          
          
          
          tapUrl = 'gameSchedule.so?method=basic&amp;gameId=G101&amp;gameRound=180056';
          
          
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '3') {
           if(whereStr !=null &amp;&amp; whereStr =='tabClick'){
                tapUrl = 'teamMatchRecord.so?method=getMatchRecordList&amp;gameId=G101&amp;innerRound=180056&amp;outerRound=56&amp;saleYear=2018';
           } else {
		       
		              
	           tapUrl = 'teamMatchRecord.so?method=getMatchRecordList&amp;gameId=G101&amp;innerRound=180056&amp;outerRound=56&amp;saleYear=2018&amp;matchSeq=&amp;selectedItem=';           
            }
           tapUrl = "worldcup2010TeamInfo.so?gameId=G101&amp;gameRound=180056";
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '4') {
           if(whereStr !=null &amp;&amp; whereStr =='tabClick'){
               tapUrl = 'analysisPanel.so?cmd=list&amp;gameId=G101&amp;gameRound=180056';
           }else {
	           
	           
	             
	           
	           tapUrl = 'analysisPanel.so?cmd=list&amp;gameId=G101&amp;gameRound=180056&amp;type=&amp;sequenceNo=&amp;page=&amp;searchType=&amp;keyWord=';
           }
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '5') {
           tapUrl = "worldcup2010ScheduleTournament.so";
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '6') {
           tapUrl = "worldcup2010RankingFifa.so";
       }
       else if (tapSeq == '7') {
    	      	   
       	   
    	   
           tapUrl = 'gameNoticeList.so?gameId=G101&amp;gameOutRound=2018/56';
           
           
       }
       
       clickGambetTab(tapSeq, tapUrl);
    }
    //--&gt;
    </script>

<!-- 게임 유형 안내 팝업 레이어  -->
<div class="popCondition popConditionUO" id="helpAboutUoGameType" style="position: absolute; top: 60px; left: 165px; z-index: 2; display:none; ">
<div>
<h1>프로토 승부식 <strong>언더오버</strong> 게임유형 안내</h1>
<a class="close" href="javascript:closeHelpLayer('helpAboutUoGameType');"><img alt="닫기" src="images/slip/btn_close405.gif"/></a>
<ol>
<li>1. 양팀 득점 총 합이 제시된 기준 값보다 <br/>    작은 값인지(언더) 큰 값인지(오버)를 예상하여 맞히는 방식</li>
<li>2. U(언더) : 제시된 기준 값보다 양팀 득점의 총 합이 작을 때<br/>    O(오버) : 제시된 기준 값보다 양팀 득점의 총 합이 클 때</li>
</ol>
<h2>예시) 축구 예시 (기준값 2.5 제시)</h2>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

<th class="thCen" colspan="2">프로토 결과</th>

<br/><span class="note">* 동일한 대상경기의 일반 승무패 / 핸디캡 / 언더오버 유형 조합 구매는 불가능합니다.</span><!-- 20140306 추가 -->

<div class="popCondition popConditionUO" id="helpAboutHandiGameType" style="position: absolute; top: 60px; left: 165px; z-index: 2; display:none; ">
<div>
<h1>프로토 승부식 <strong>핸디캡</strong> 게임유형 안내</h1>
<a class="close" href="javascript:closeHelpLayer('helpAboutHandiGameType');"><img alt="닫기" src="images/slip/btn_close405.gif"/></a>
<ol>
<li>1. 주어진 조건(핸디캡)을 반영한 홈팀 승/무/패 결과를 예상하여 맞히는 방식</li>
<li>2. 핸디캡(H) - 일반적으로 강팀에게 핸디캡(-), 약팀에게 어드벤티지(+) 적용</li>
</ol>

<h1>프로토 승부식 <strong>일반</strong> 게임유형 안내</h1>
<a class="close" href="javascript:closeHelpLayer('helpAboutNomalGameType');"><img alt="닫기" src="images/slip/btn_close405.gif"/></a>
<ol>
<li>1. 홈팀 승/무/패 결과를 예상하여 맞히는 방식</li>
<li>2.승 = 홈팀 승 / 무 = 무승부 / 패 = 홈팀 패</li>
</ol>
